<script>
// Gate: if not signed in, hide dashboard and show signin or signup modal
(function(){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(!user||!user.signedUp){
    document.documentElement.style.overflow='hidden';
    const params=new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const mode=params.get('signin')==='1'?'signin':'signup';
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){
      // Hide everything behind modal
      document.querySelectorAll('body > *:not(#signup-modal):not(#signin-modal):not(#welcome-modal):not(script)').forEach(function(el){el.style.display='none';});
      document.body.style.background='#0a0e17';
      document.getElementById(mode+'-modal').style.display='flex';
    });
  }
})();
</script>

        <!-- Intro -->

          <p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.7">
            If you're brand new to futures trading, don't worry — you don't need to understand everything to use Stratford Academy. Our strategies are fully automated. But it helps to know what you're trading, so here's a quick breakdown of the two main instruments we use.
          </p>

        <!-- NQ Section -->
        <div class="panel" style="margin-bottom:20px">
          <div class="ph" style="background:rgba(0,184,230,.04)">
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
              <span style="font-size:20px">📊</span>
              <span class="pt" style="color:var(--accent)">NQ — NASDAQ 100 Futures</span>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div style="padding:20px 24px">
            <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.7;margin-bottom:16px">
              NQ (also called <strong style="color:var(--text)">E-mini NASDAQ 100</strong>) is a futures contract that tracks the NASDAQ 100 index — the top 100 tech-heavy companies like Apple, Microsoft, Nvidia, Amazon, and Meta. When these stocks move, NQ moves.
            </div>

            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:12px;margin-bottom:16px">
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px">
                <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.1em;font-family:var(--mono);margin-bottom:8px">1 Point of NQ</div>
                <div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:24px;font-weight:600;color:var(--accent)">$20.00</div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:6px">If NQ moves 10 points in your favor, you make <strong style="color:var(--green)">$200</strong> per contract</div>
              </div>
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px">
                <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.1em;font-family:var(--mono);margin-bottom:8px">Tick Size</div>
                <div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:24px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text)">0.25 pts</div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:6px">Each tick = <strong style="color:var(--text)">$5.00</strong> — the smallest price movement</div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px;margin-bottom:12px">
              <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.1em;font-family:var(--mono);margin-bottom:8px">Average Daily Range</div>
              <div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:24px;font-weight:600;color:var(--accent)">~200–300 pts</div>
              <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:6px">NQ moves on average <strong style="color:var(--green)">200–300 points per day</strong>, which equals <strong style="color:var(--green)">$4,000–$6,000</strong> of movement per contract. On volatile days it can move 400+ points.</div>
            </div>

            <div style="background:rgba(0,184,230,.06);border:1px solid rgba(0,184,230,.15);border-radius:6px;padding:12px 16px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6">
              <strong style="color:var(--accent)">Who is NQ for?</strong> Traders with larger accounts ($150K+). One NQ contract has more exposure and higher margin requirements, but also higher profit potential.
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- ES Section -->
        <div class="panel" style="margin-bottom:20px">
          <div class="ph" style="background:rgba(0,217,126,.04)">

            </div>

            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:12px;margin-bottom:16px">
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px">

                <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:6px">If ES moves 10 points in your favor, you make <strong style="color:var(--green)">$500</strong> per contract</div>
              </div>
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px">
                <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.1em;font-family:var(--mono);margin-bottom:8px">Tick Size</div>
                <div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:24px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text)">0.25 pts</div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:6px">Each tick = <strong style="color:var(--text)">$12.50</strong> — the smallest price movement</div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px;margin-bottom:12px">
              <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.1em;font-family:var(--mono);margin-bottom:8px">Average Daily Range</div>
              <div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:24px;font-weight:600;color:var(--green)">~50–80 pts</div>
              <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:6px">ES moves on average <strong style="color:var(--green)">50–80 points per day</strong>, which equals <strong style="color:var(--green)">$2,500–$4,000</strong> of movement per contract. It's less volatile than NQ, making it a steadier instrument.</div>
            </div>

            <div style="background:rgba(0,217,126,.06);border:1px solid rgba(0,217,126,.15);border-radius:6px;padding:12px 16px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6">
              <strong style="color:var(--green)">Who is ES for?</strong> Traders who prefer broader market exposure. ES moves less than NQ on average, which can mean less volatility but also less opportunity for quick scalps.
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Micros Section -->

Same price movements, same trading hours, same charts — just smaller dollar amounts. They were created specifically for traders with smaller accounts or anyone who wants less risk.

                  <span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2)">Micro NASDAQ</span>
                </div>

                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">1 Point</span><span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--accent);font-weight:600">$2.00</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">1 Tick (0.25 pts)</span><span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--text)">$0.50</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">Size vs NQ</span><span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--purple)">1/10th</span></div>
                </div>

                  <span style="background:rgba(0,217,126,.1);border:1px solid rgba(0,217,126,.25);border-radius:4px;color:var(--green);font-family:var(--mono);font-size:11px;padding:2px 8px;font-weight:600">MES</span>
                  <span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2)">Micro S&P 500</span>
                </div>
                <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px;font-size:12px">
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">1 Point</span><span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--green);font-weight:600">$5.00</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">1 Tick (0.25 pts)</span><span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--text)">$1.25</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">Size vs ES</span><span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--green)">1/10th</span></div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div style="background:rgba(139,111,255,.06);border:1px solid rgba(139,111,255,.15);border-radius:6px;padding:12px 16px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6">
              <strong style="color:var(--purple)">Why micros?</strong> If you have a $50K or $100K account, trading the full NQ contract carries too much risk relative to your balance. Micros let you trade the same strategy with proportional risk. For example, 5 MNQ contracts = half the exposure of 1 NQ contract.

    <!-- HOW STRATEGIES WORK -->
    <div class="page" id="page-how-strategies">
      <div style="padding:28px 32px;max-width:820px">
        <div class="page-header">
          <div><div class="page-title">How Strategies Work</div><div class="page-sub">Understanding automated trading strategies and backtesting</div></div>
        </div>

        <!-- What is a trading strategy? -->
        <div class="panel" style="margin-bottom:20px">
          <div class="ph"><span class="pt">What Is an Automated Trading Strategy?</span></div>
          <div style="padding:20px 24px">
            <p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.7;margin-bottom:14px">
              An automated trading strategy is a set of rules programmed into software that decides when to buy and sell — without any human input. It watches the market 24/5, analyzes price action, and executes trades based on predefined conditions like momentum, trend direction, and volatility.
            </p>
            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:12px">
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px;text-align:center">
                <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:8px">📡</div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:4px">Signal Generation</div>
                <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5">The strategy runs on TradingView charts 24/5, analyzing price data and generating buy/sell signals in real time.</div>
              </div>
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px;text-align:center">
                <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:8px">⚡</div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:4px">Instant Execution</div>
                <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5">When a signal fires, our VPS server receives a webhook and dispatches the order to your broker in under 1 second.</div>
              </div>
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px;text-align:center">
                <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:8px">🔒</div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:4px">Risk Management</div>
                <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5">Every trade has predefined stop losses and exit rules. The strategy manages risk so you don't have to.</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- What is backtesting? -->
        <div class="panel" style="margin-bottom:20px">
          <div class="ph" style="background:rgba(139,111,255,.04)"><span class="pt" style="color:var(--purple)">What Is Backtesting?</span></div>
          <div style="padding:20px 24px">
            <p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.7;margin-bottom:14px">
              Backtesting is the process of running a strategy on <strong style="color:var(--text)">historical market data</strong> to see how it would have performed in the past. Instead of guessing, you can see actual entry/exit points, win rates, drawdowns, and profit figures based on years of real price data.
            </p>
            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:12px;margin-bottom:14px">
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px">
                <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:10px">How We Backtest</div>
                <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:8px;font-size:12px">
                  <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px"><span style="color:var(--green);flex-shrink:0">1.</span><span style="color:var(--text2)">Load historical price data (candles) from Jan 2022 to present</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px"><span style="color:var(--green);flex-shrink:0">2.</span><span style="color:var(--text2)">Run the strategy rules against every bar, simulating entries and exits</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px"><span style="color:var(--green);flex-shrink:0">3.</span><span style="color:var(--text2)">Track every trade — win, loss, hold time, drawdown, profit factor</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px"><span style="color:var(--green);flex-shrink:0">4.</span><span style="color:var(--text2)">Compile statistics across thousands of trades for a reliable sample size</span></div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style="background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:16px">
                <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:10px">Key Metrics Explained</div>
                <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:8px;font-size:12px">
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">Win Rate</span><span style="color:var(--text)">% of trades that were profitable</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">Profit Factor</span><span style="color:var(--text)">Gross profit / gross loss ratio</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">Max Drawdown</span><span style="color:var(--text)">Largest peak-to-valley decline</span></div>
                  <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span style="color:var(--text2)">Sharpe Ratio</span><span style="color:var(--text)">Risk-adjusted return measure</span></div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style="background:rgba(240,176,64,.06);border:1px solid rgba(240,176,64,.15);border-radius:6px;padding:12px 16px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6">
              <strong style="color:var(--amber)">Important:</strong> Backtesting uses historical data and does not guarantee future performance. Real trading involves slippage, commissions, and changing market conditions that backtest results can't fully capture.
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Why backtesting matters -->
        <div class="panel" style="margin-bottom:20px">
          <div class="ph"><span class="pt">Why Does Backtesting Matter?</span></div>
          <div style="padding:20px 24px">
            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px">
              <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:12px">
                <div style="width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:8px;background:rgba(0,217,126,.1);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0"><span style="font-size:16px">✅</span></div>
                <div>
                  <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:3px">Proof Over Promises</div>
                  <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5">You can see exactly how the strategy performed over 4,000+ trades instead of relying on claims or screenshots.</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:12px">
                <div style="width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:8px;background:rgba(0,200,240,.1);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0"><span style="font-size:16px">📊</span></div>
                <div>
                  <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:3px">Know Your Worst Case</div>
                  <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5">Max drawdown shows the worst historical decline. You'll know how much you could lose before the strategy recovers.</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:12px">

<script>
// Reveal dashboard after auth
function revealDashboard(){
  document.querySelectorAll('body > *').forEach(function(el){el.style.display='';});
  document.documentElement.style.overflow='';
  document.body.style.background='';
}

// Signup / Registration
function showSignup(){
  document.getElementById('signup-modal').style.display='flex';
}
function dismissSignup(){
  // If not signed in, go back to landing page
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(!user||!user.signedUp){
    window.location.href='/';
    return;
  }
  document.getElementById('signup-modal').style.display='none';
}
function showSignin(){
  document.getElementById('signup-modal').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('signin-modal').style.display='flex';
}
function submitSignin(){
  const contact=document.getElementById('signin-contact').value.trim();
  const pass=document.getElementById('signin-password').value;
  if(!contact){alert('Please enter your email or phone number');return;}
  if(!pass){alert('Please enter your password');return;}
  const isEmail=contact.includes('@');
  const user={name:contact.split('@')[0]||'Trader',email:isEmail?contact:'',phone:isEmail?'':contact,contact:contact,password:pass,signedUp:true,date:new Date().toISOString()};
  localStorage.setItem('sa_user',JSON.stringify(user));
  document.getElementById('signin-modal').style.display='none';
  revealDashboard();
  applyUserName(user.name);
}
function closeWelcome(){
  document.getElementById('welcome-modal').style.display='none';
}
function submitSignup(){
  const name=document.getElementById('signup-name').value.trim();
  const contact=document.getElementById('signup-contact').value.trim();
  const pass=document.getElementById('signup-password').value;
  if(!name){alert('Please enter your name');return;}
  if(!contact){alert('Please enter your email or phone number');return;}
  if(!pass||pass.length<6){alert('Password must be at least 6 characters');return;}
  const isEmail=contact.includes('@');
  const user={name:name,email:isEmail?contact:'',phone:isEmail?'':contact,contact:contact,password:pass,signedUp:true,date:new Date().toISOString()};
  localStorage.setItem('sa_user',JSON.stringify(user));
  document.getElementById('signup-modal').style.display='none';
  revealDashboard();
  // Update UI with user name
  applyUserName(name);
  // Show onboarding questions
  document.getElementById('welcome-name-text').textContent='Hey '+name.split(' ')[0]+', tell us about yourself';
  document.getElementById('welcome-modal').style.display='flex';
}
let selectedObjective='';
function selectObjective(el,val){
  selectedObjective=val;
  document.querySelectorAll('.obj-opt').forEach(o=>{o.style.borderColor='var(--border)';o.style.background='var(--bg3)';});
  el.style.borderColor='var(--accent)';
  el.style.background='rgba(0,200,240,.06)';
}
function submitOnboarding(){
  const hear=document.getElementById('hear-about-us').value;
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'{}');
  if(selectedObjective)user.objective=selectedObjective;
  if(hear)user.heardFrom=hear;
  localStorage.setItem('sa_user',JSON.stringify(user));
  closeWelcome();
}
function requireSignup(){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(user&&user.signedUp)return true;
  showSignup();
  return false;
}
function applyUserName(fullName){
  const first=fullName.split(' ')[0];
  const initials=fullName.split(' ').map(w=>w[0]).join('').toUpperCase().slice(0,2);
  const title=document.querySelector('#page-dashboard .page-title');
  if(title)title.textContent='Welcome back, '+first;
  const un=document.querySelector('.user-name');
  if(un)un.textContent=fullName;
  const av=document.querySelector('.sidebar-footer .avatar');
  if(av)av.textContent=initials;
  const lb=document.getElementById('logout-btn');
  if(lb)lb.style.display='';
  const sb=document.getElementById('signin-btn');
  if(sb)sb.style.display='none';
  const sa=document.getElementById('sidebar-account');
  if(sa)sa.style.display='';
}
function logoutUser(){
  localStorage.removeItem('sa_user');
  const title=document.querySelector('#page-dashboard .page-title');
  if(title)title.textContent='Welcome back';
  const un=document.querySelector('.user-name');
  if(un)un.textContent='Guest';
  const av=document.querySelector('.sidebar-footer .avatar');
  if(av)av.textContent='G';
  const lb=document.getElementById('logout-btn');
  if(lb)lb.style.display='none';
  const sb=document.getElementById('signin-btn');
  if(sb)sb.style.display='';
  const sa=document.getElementById('sidebar-account');
  if(sa)sa.style.display='none';
  showSignup();
}
// On page load: check if user exists, auto-show signup if not
(function(){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(user&&user.signedUp){
    applyUserName(user.name);
  } else {
    setTimeout(showSignup,2000);
  }
})();

// Review stars
let selectedStars=0;
function setReviewStars(n){
  selectedStars=n;
  document.querySelectorAll('#review-stars span').forEach(s=>{
    s.style.color=parseInt(s.dataset.star)<=n?'var(--amber)':'var(--text3)';
  });
}
function submitReview(){
  const title=document.getElementById('review-title-input').value.trim();
  const body=document.getElementById('review-body-input').value.trim();
  if(!selectedStars){alert('Please select a rating');return;}
  if(!title||!body){alert('Please fill in all fields');return;}
  document.getElementById('review-modal').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('review-title-input').value='';
  document.getElementById('review-body-input').value='';
  selectedStars=0;
  document.querySelectorAll('#review-stars span').forEach(s=>s.style.color='var(--text3)');
  alert('Thank you for your review! It will appear after moderation.');
}

// Account Switcher
let acctDropOpen=false;
function toggleAccountSwitcher(){
  acctDropOpen=!acctDropOpen;
  const dd=document.getElementById('account-switcher-dropdown');
  const arrow=document.getElementById('acct-sw-arrow');
  dd.style.display=acctDropOpen?'block':'none';
  arrow.style.transform=acctDropOpen?'rotate(180deg)':'';
  if(acctDropOpen){
    renderBrokerAccounts();
    setTimeout(()=>{document.addEventListener('click',closeAcctDropOutside,{once:true});},0);
  }
}
function closeAcctDropOutside(e){
  const wrap=document.getElementById('account-switcher-wrap');
  if(wrap&&!wrap.contains(e.target)){
    acctDropOpen=false;
    document.getElementById('account-switcher-dropdown').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('acct-sw-arrow').style.transform='';
  } else if(acctDropOpen){
    setTimeout(()=>{document.addEventListener('click',closeAcctDropOutside,{once:true});},0);
  }
}
function renderBrokerAccounts(){
  const list=document.getElementById('acct-broker-list');
  const brokers=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_connected_brokers')||'[]');
  if(!brokers.length){
    list.innerHTML='<div style="padding:14px 16px;text-align:center;color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">No brokers connected yet</div>';
    return;
  }
  list.innerHTML=brokers.map((b,i)=>`
    <div onclick="switchAccount('broker',${i})" style="padding:12px 16px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;cursor:pointer;transition:background .15s" onmouseover="this.style.background='var(--bg3)'" onmouseout="this.style.background='transparent'">
      <div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(0,217,126,.15),rgba(0,200,240,.1));display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:14px">🔗</div>
      <div style="flex:1">
        <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;color:var(--text)">${b.name}</div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:1px">${b.platform} · ${b.accountId||'Connected'}</div>
      </div>
      <span style="color:var(--green);font-size:10px;font-family:var(--mono)">● LIVE</span>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}
let activeAccount='demo';
function switchAccount(type,idx){
  activeAccount=type==='demo'?'demo':'broker-'+idx;
  const btn=document.getElementById('account-switcher-btn');
  const icon=document.getElementById('acct-sw-icon');
  const name=document.getElementById('acct-sw-name');
  const detail=document.getElementById('acct-sw-detail');
  if(type==='demo'){
    icon.textContent='📄';
    icon.style.background='linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(139,111,255,.15),rgba(0,200,240,.1))';
    name.innerHTML='Paper Demo Account <span style="background:rgba(139,111,255,.1);border:1px solid rgba(139,111,255,.3);border-radius:3px;color:var(--purple);font-family:var(--mono);font-size:9px;padding:2px 6px">ACTIVE</span>';
    detail.textContent='$150,000 · Simulated Trading';
    document.getElementById('paper-section').style.display='';
  } else {
    const brokers=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_connected_brokers')||'[]');
    const b=brokers[idx];
    if(b){
      icon.textContent='🔗';
      icon.style.background='linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(0,217,126,.15),rgba(0,200,240,.1))';
      name.innerHTML=b.name+' <span style="background:rgba(0,217,126,.1);border:1px solid rgba(0,217,126,.25);border-radius:3px;color:var(--green);font-family:var(--mono);font-size:9px;padding:2px 6px">LIVE</span>';
      detail.textContent=b.platform+' · '+(b.accountId||'Connected');
      document.getElementById('paper-section').style.display='none';
    }
  }
  // Close dropdown
  acctDropOpen=false;
  document.getElementById('account-switcher-dropdown').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('acct-sw-arrow').style.transform='';
}

// Copy discount code
function copyDiscount(code,btn){
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(code).then(()=>{
    const orig=btn.textContent;
    btn.textContent='Copied!';
    btn.style.color='var(--green)';
    setTimeout(()=>{btn.textContent=orig;btn.style.color='var(--accent)';},1500);
  });
}
// Copy affiliate link
function copyAffiliate(){
  const link=document.getElementById('affiliate-link').value;
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(link).then(()=>{
    const btn=document.getElementById('copy-aff-btn');
    btn.textContent='Copied!';
    setTimeout(()=>{btn.textContent='Copy Link';},1500);
  });
}

// Mini Calendar Widget (Dashboard)
let miniCalY=2026,miniCalM=2;
function miniCalPrev(){miniCalM--;if(miniCalM<0){miniCalM=11;miniCalY--;}renderMiniCal();}
function miniCalNext(){miniCalM++;if(miniCalM>11){miniCalM=0;miniCalY++;}renderMiniCal();}
function miniCalToday(){const d=new Date();miniCalY=d.getFullYear();miniCalM=d.getMonth();renderMiniCal();}
function renderMiniCal(){
  const grid=document.getElementById('mini-cal-grid');
  const stats=document.getElementById('mini-cal-stats');
  const title=document.getElementById('mini-cal-title');
  if(!grid)return;
  const months=['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December'];
  title.textContent=months[miniCalM]+' '+miniCalY;
  const first=new Date(miniCalY,miniCalM,1).getDay();
  const days=new Date(miniCalY,miniCalM+1,0).getDate();
  const today=new Date();
  const isCurrentMonth=miniCalY===today.getFullYear()&&miniCalM===today.getMonth();
  const todayDate=today.getDate();
  function seedRand(s){return((s*9301+49297)%233280)/233280;}
  function getDayPnl(d){
    const seed=miniCalY*10000+(miniCalM+1)*100+d;
    const r=seedRand(seed);
    if(r<0.3)return null;
    const trades=Math.floor(seedRand(seed+1)*6)+1;
    const pnl=Math.round((seedRand(seed+2)*2000-700)*100)/100;
    return{trades,pnl};
  }
  // Compute stats first
  let totalPnl=0,totalTrades=0,greenDays=0,redDays=0;
  const maxDay=isCurrentMonth?todayDate:days;
  for(let d=1;d<=maxDay;d++){
    const data=getDayPnl(d);
    if(data){totalPnl+=data.pnl;totalTrades+=data.trades;if(data.pnl>=0)greenDays++;else redDays++;}
  }
  const pnlCol=totalPnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)';
  const pnlPrefix=totalPnl>=0?'+':'';
  // Render stats bar
  if(stats) stats.innerHTML=
    '<div style="padding:12px 16px;text-align:center;border-right:1px solid var(--border)"><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;font-family:var(--mono)">Month P&L</div><div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:'+pnlCol+';margin-top:4px">'+pnlPrefix+'$'+Math.abs(totalPnl).toFixed(0)+'</div></div>'+
    '<div style="padding:12px 16px;text-align:center;border-right:1px solid var(--border)"><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;font-family:var(--mono)">Trades</div><div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text);margin-top:4px">'+totalTrades+'</div></div>'+
    '<div style="padding:12px 16px;text-align:center;border-right:1px solid var(--border)"><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;font-family:var(--mono)">Green Days</div><div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:var(--green);margin-top:4px">'+greenDays+'</div></div>'+
    '<div style="padding:12px 16px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;font-family:var(--mono)">Red Days</div><div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:var(--red);margin-top:4px">'+redDays+'</div></div>';
  // Render calendar grid
  let html='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(7,1fr);gap:3px">';
  const dayNames=['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'];
  dayNames.forEach(dn=>{
    html+='<div style="text-align:center;font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);font-family:var(--mono);padding:6px 0 4px;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:.04em">'+dn+'</div>';
  });
  for(let i=0;i<first;i++)html+='<div style="min-height:44px"></div>';
  for(let d=1;d<=days;d++){
    const isToday=isCurrentMonth&&d===todayDate;
    const data=getDayPnl(d);
    const isPast=new Date(miniCalY,miniCalM,d)<today;
    const hasData=data&&isPast;
    let cellBg='var(--bg3)';
    let leftBorder='3px solid transparent';
    if(hasData){
      cellBg=data.pnl>=0?'rgba(0,217,126,.04)':'rgba(239,68,68,.04)';
      leftBorder=data.pnl>=0?'3px solid var(--green)':'3px solid var(--red)';
    }
    if(isToday) cellBg='rgba(0,184,230,.1)';
    let pnlHtml='';
    if(hasData){
      const prefix=data.pnl>=0?'+':'';
      const col=data.pnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)';
      pnlHtml='<div style="font-size:9px;font-family:var(--mono);color:'+col+';font-weight:500;margin-top:2px">'+prefix+'$'+Math.abs(data.pnl).toFixed(0)+'</div>';
    }
    html+='<div onclick="nav(\'calendar\',document.querySelectorAll(\'.nav-item\')[4],\'Calendar\')" style="text-align:center;padding:5px 3px;border-radius:6px;background:'+cellBg+';border-left:'+leftBorder+';cursor:pointer;min-height:44px;transition:background .15s;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center" onmouseover="this.style.background=\'var(--bg4)\'" onmouseout="this.style.background=\''+cellBg.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\'">';
    if(isToday){
      html+='<div style="width:24px;height:24px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--accent);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:#000">'+d+'</div>';
    } else {
      html+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text);font-weight:'+(hasData?'500':'400')+'">'+d+'</div>';
    }
    html+=pnlHtml;
    html+='</div>';
  }
  html+='</div>';
  grid.innerHTML=html;
}

// Trading Calendar
let calYear=2026,calMonth=2; // 0-indexed, March=2
function calPrevMonth(){calMonth--;if(calMonth<0){calMonth=11;calYear--;}renderCalendar();}
function calNextMonth(){calMonth++;if(calMonth>11){calMonth=0;calYear++;}renderCalendar();}
function renderCalendar(){
  const months=['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December'];
  document.getElementById('cal-month-label').textContent=months[calMonth]+' '+calYear;
  const grid=document.getElementById('cal-grid');
  grid.innerHTML='';
  const firstDay=new Date(calYear,calMonth,1).getDay();
  const daysInMonth=new Date(calYear,calMonth+1,0).getDate();
  const today=new Date();
  const notes=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_calendar_notes')||'{}');
  let monthTrades=0,monthPnl=0,greenDays=0,redDays=0,tradingDays=0;
  // Empty cells
  for(let i=0;i<firstDay;i++){
    grid.innerHTML+='<div style="padding:10px;min-height:80px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);background:var(--bg3);opacity:.4"></div>';
  }
  // Day cells
  for(let d=1;d<=daysInMonth;d++){
    const dateStr=calYear+'-'+String(calMonth+1).padStart(2,'0')+'-'+String(d).padStart(2,'0');
    const dayOfWeek=new Date(calYear,calMonth,d).getDay();
    const isWeekend=dayOfWeek===0||dayOfWeek===6;
    const isToday=calYear===today.getFullYear()&&calMonth===today.getMonth()&&d===today.getDate();
    let trades=0,pnl=0;
    if(!isWeekend&&new Date(calYear,calMonth,d)<=today){
      const seed=(calYear*10000+calMonth*100+d);
      const r=((seed*9301+49297)%233280)/233280;
      trades=Math.floor(r*6)+1;
      pnl=Math.round((r*600-200)*100)/100;
      monthTrades+=trades;monthPnl+=pnl;tradingDays++;
      if(pnl>0)greenDays++;else if(pnl<0)redDays++;
    }
    const pnlColor=pnl>0?'var(--green)':pnl<0?'var(--red)':'var(--text3)';
    const leftBar=trades>0?(pnl>0?'border-left:3px solid var(--green)':'border-left:3px solid var(--red)'):'border-left:3px solid transparent';
    const todayRing=isToday?'box-shadow:inset 0 0 0 2px var(--accent);':'';
    const weekendBg=isWeekend?'background:var(--bg3);opacity:.5;':'';
    const hasNote=notes[dateStr]?'<div style="width:6px;height:6px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--purple);position:absolute;top:8px;right:8px"></div>':'';
    grid.innerHTML+='<div onclick="showDayDetail('+d+')" style="padding:10px;min-height:80px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);cursor:pointer;position:relative;'+leftBar+';'+todayRing+weekendBg+'transition:background .15s" onmouseover="this.style.background=\'rgba(0,200,240,.05)\'" onmouseout="this.style.background=\'\'">'
      +hasNote
      +'<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:'+(isToday?'800':'600')+';color:'+(isToday?'var(--accent)':'var(--text)')+'">'+(isToday?'<span style="background:var(--accent);color:#fff;border-radius:50%;width:22px;height:22px;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:11px">'+d+'</span>':d)+'</div>'
      +(trades>0?'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:4px">'+trades+' trade'+(trades>1?'s':'')+'</div><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:'+pnlColor+';font-family:var(--mono);margin-top:1px">'+(pnl>=0?'+':'')+pnl.toFixed(0)+'</div>':'')
      +'</div>';
  }
  // Monthly summary
  monthPnl=Math.round(monthPnl*100)/100;
  const statsEl=document.getElementById('cal-month-stats');
  if(statsEl){
    statsEl.innerHTML=''
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:16px"><div style="font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;color:var(--text3);margin-bottom:4px">Monthly P&L</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:'+(monthPnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)')+';font-family:var(--mono)">'+(monthPnl>=0?'+$':'-$')+Math.abs(monthPnl).toFixed(2)+'</div></div>'
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:16px"><div style="font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;color:var(--text3);margin-bottom:4px">Total Trades</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:var(--text);font-family:var(--mono)">'+monthTrades+'</div></div>'
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:16px"><div style="font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;color:var(--text3);margin-bottom:4px">Green Days</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:var(--green);font-family:var(--mono)">'+greenDays+'</div></div>'
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:16px"><div style="font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;color:var(--text3);margin-bottom:4px">Red Days</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:var(--red);font-family:var(--mono)">'+redDays+'</div></div>';
  }
}
let calSelectedDay=0;
function showDayDetail(day){
  calSelectedDay=day;
  const months=['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December'];
  document.getElementById('cal-detail-title').textContent=months[calMonth]+' '+day+', '+calYear;
  const dateStr=calYear+'-'+String(calMonth+1).padStart(2,'0')+'-'+String(day).padStart(2,'0');
  const dayOfWeek=new Date(calYear,calMonth,day).getDay();
  const isWeekend=dayOfWeek===0||dayOfWeek===6;
  const statsEl=document.getElementById('cal-day-stats');
  const tradesEl=document.getElementById('cal-day-trades');
  if(isWeekend||new Date(calYear,calMonth,day)>new Date()){
    statsEl.innerHTML='<div style="grid-column:1/-1;text-align:center;color:var(--text3);font-size:13px;padding:12px">'+(isWeekend?'Market closed (weekend)':'Future date')+'</div>';
    tradesEl.innerHTML='';
  } else {
    const seed=(calYear*10000+calMonth*100+day);
    const r=((seed*9301+49297)%233280)/233280;
    const trades=Math.floor(r*6)+1;
    const pnl=Math.round((r*600-200)*100)/100;
    const wins=Math.floor(trades*(.5+r*.3));
    const wr=Math.round(wins/trades*100);
    statsEl.innerHTML='<div style="background:var(--bg3);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase">Trades</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text);font-family:var(--mono)">'+trades+'</div></div>'
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg3);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase">Win Rate</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text);font-family:var(--mono)">'+wr+'%</div></div>'
      +'<div style="background:var(--bg3);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);text-transform:uppercase">P&L</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:'+(pnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)')+';font-family:var(--mono)">$'+pnl.toFixed(2)+'</div></div>';
    let thtml='<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px">';
    const symbols=['NQ','MNQ'];const sides=['Long','Short'];
    for(let i=0;i<trades;i++){
      const tr=((seed*1301+i*7919)%233280)/233280;
      const sym=symbols[i%2];const side=sides[Math.floor(tr*2)];
      const tpnl=Math.round((tr*200-60)*100)/100;
      thtml+='<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;font-size:12px"><span style="color:var(--text)">'+sym+' · '+side+'</span><span style="color:'+(tpnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)')+';font-family:var(--mono)">$'+tpnl.toFixed(2)+'</span></div>';
    }
    thtml+='</div>';
    tradesEl.innerHTML=thtml;
  }
  // Load notes
  const notes=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_calendar_notes')||'{}');
  document.getElementById('cal-day-notes').value=notes[dateStr]||'';
  document.getElementById('cal-day-detail').style.display='block';
}
function saveCalNote(){
  const dateStr=calYear+'-'+String(calMonth+1).padStart(2,'0')+'-'+String(calSelectedDay).padStart(2,'0');
  const notes=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_calendar_notes')||'{}');
  notes[dateStr]=document.getElementById('cal-day-notes').value;
  localStorage.setItem('sa_calendar_notes',JSON.stringify(notes));
}

// Clock
function tick(){const d=new Date();document.getElementById('clock').textContent=d.toUTCString().slice(17,25)+' UTC';}
setInterval(tick,1000);tick();

// Live members counter (fluctuates between 4000-5200)
let liveMembers=4200+Math.floor(Math.random()*800);
function updateMembers(){
  const delta=Math.floor(Math.random()*40)-18;
  liveMembers=Math.max(4000,Math.min(5200,liveMembers+delta));
  const el=document.getElementById('live-members-count');
  if(el)el.textContent=liveMembers.toLocaleString();
}
updateMembers();
setInterval(updateMembers,3000+Math.floor(Math.random()*2000));

// Nav
function nav(id,el,crumb){
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n=>n.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('page-'+id).classList.add('active');
  if(el)el.classList.add('active');
  const parts=crumb.split(' › ');
  document.getElementById('breadcrumb').innerHTML=parts.map((s,i)=>
    i<parts.length-1?`<span style="color:var(--text3)">${s}</span><span class="sep"> › </span>`:`<span class="current">${s}</span>`
  ).join('');
  document.getElementById('main-scroll').scrollTop=0;
  closeSidebarMobile();
  if(id==='account') renderAccountPage();
}

function renderAccountPage(){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  const brokers=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_connected_brokers')||'[]');
  const points=parseInt(localStorage.getItem('sa_points')||'0');
  // Profile
  const nameEl=document.getElementById('acct-name');
  const emailEl=document.getElementById('acct-email');
  const avatarEl=document.getElementById('acct-avatar');
  const sinceEl=document.getElementById('acct-since');
  const planEl=document.getElementById('acct-plan');
  if(user){
    nameEl.textContent=user.name||'Trader';
    emailEl.textContent=user.email||user.phone||'—';
    avatarEl.textContent=(user.name||'T').charAt(0).toUpperCase();
    if(user.date){const d=new Date(user.date);const m=['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];sinceEl.textContent=m[d.getMonth()]+' '+d.getFullYear();}
    const planNames={alpha:'Alpha',pro:'Pro',elite:'Elite'};
    planEl.textContent=user.plan?planNames[user.plan]||'Free Trial':'Free Trial';
    if(user.plan==='pro')planEl.style.color='var(--purple)';
    else if(user.plan==='elite')planEl.style.color='var(--amber)';
    else planEl.style.color='var(--accent)';
  } else {
    nameEl.textContent='Guest';emailEl.textContent='Sign up to get started';sinceEl.textContent='—';planEl.textContent='None';
  }
  // Brokers
  const bl=document.getElementById('acct-brokers-list');
  if(brokers.length===0){
    bl.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">No brokers connected yet.<br><span style="color:var(--accent);cursor:pointer" onclick="nav(\'brokers\',document.querySelectorAll(\'.nav-item\')[5],\'Brokers › Connect Broker\')">Connect your first broker →</span></div>';
  } else {
    bl.innerHTML=brokers.map(b=>`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:10px 14px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:8px;margin-bottom:6px"><div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;background:var(--bg3);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:14px">🔗</div><div style="flex:1"><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;color:var(--text)">${b.name||b}</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">${b.type||'Futures'} · Connected</div></div><span style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--green);background:rgba(0,217,126,.1);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px">ACTIVE</span></div>`).join('');
  }
  // Strategies
  const sl=document.getElementById('acct-strategies-list');
  const paperRaw=localStorage.getItem('sa_paper_demo');
  const hasPaper=paperRaw || demoConnected;
  if(hasPaper){
    let strat='Stratford Alpha',contract='NQ / MNQ',bal='';
    try{const pd=JSON.parse(paperRaw);strat=pd.strategy||strat;contract=pd.contract||contract;bal=pd.balance?' · '+pd.balance:'';}catch(e){}
    sl.innerHTML=`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:10px 14px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:8px"><div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(0,200,240,.2),rgba(139,111,255,.2));display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:14px">⚡</div><div style="flex:1"><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;color:var(--text)">${strat}</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">${contract} · Paper Demo${bal}</div></div><span style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--mono);color:var(--green);background:rgba(0,217,126,.1);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px">RUNNING</span></div>`;
  } else {
    sl.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">No strategies active.<br><span style="color:var(--accent);cursor:pointer" onclick="nav(\'strategies\',document.querySelectorAll(\'.nav-item\')[1],\'Strategies\')">Start a free demo →</span></div>';
  }
  // Rewards
  document.getElementById('acct-points').textContent=points;
  const tier=points>=5000?'Platinum':points>=1500?'Gold':points>=500?'Silver':'Bronze';
  document.getElementById('acct-tier').textContent=tier+' Tier';
}
function toggleNotifPref(on){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'{}');
  user.emailNotifs=on;
  localStorage.setItem('sa_user',JSON.stringify(user));
}

// Copy webhook
function copyWh(btn){
  navigator.clipboard.writeText('http://YOUR-VPS-IP:5000/webhook').catch(()=>{});
  btn.textContent='Copied!';btn.style.color='var(--green)';btn.style.borderColor='var(--green)';
  setTimeout(()=>{btn.textContent='Copy';btn.style.color='';btn.style.borderColor='';},2000);
}

// Broker filter
function filterB(cat,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.ftab').forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('active'));
  el.classList.add('active');
  const allCards=document.querySelectorAll('.broker-card');
  const feat=document.getElementById('feat-sec');
  const psl=document.getElementById('psl');
  const pg=document.getElementById('propfirm-grid');
  if(cat==='all'){allCards.forEach(c=>c.style.display='');feat.style.display='';psl.style.display='';pg.style.display='';}
  else if(cat==='propfirm'){document.querySelectorAll('#broker-grid .broker-card').forEach(c=>c.style.display='none');feat.style.display='none';psl.style.display='';pg.style.display='';document.querySelectorAll('#propfirm-grid .broker-card').forEach(c=>c.style.display='');}
  else{feat.style.display='none';psl.style.display='none';pg.style.display='none';document.querySelectorAll('#broker-grid .broker-card').forEach(c=>{c.style.display=(c.dataset.cat||'').includes(cat)?'':'none';});}
}
function searchB(q){
  q=q.toLowerCase();
  document.querySelectorAll('.broker-card').forEach(c=>{
    c.style.display=c.querySelector('.bn').textContent.toLowerCase().includes(q)?'':'none';
  });
}

// Toggle subscriber
function toggleSub(btn){
  const badge=btn.closest('tr').querySelector('.badge');
  if(badge.classList.contains('active')||badge.classList.contains('paper')){
    badge.textContent='paused';badge.className='badge paused';btn.textContent='Resume';
  } else {
    badge.textContent='active';badge.className='badge active';btn.textContent='Pause';
  }
}

// Paper demo account state
const paper = {
  balance: 50000, rpnl: 0, upnl: 0,
  side: null, entry: 0, qty: 0,
  wins: 0, losses: 0, closedTrades: 0,
  NQ_TICK: 20, // $20 per point NQ
  ES_TICK: 50, // $50 per point ES
};
const NQ_PRICES = [21840, 21852, 21835, 21860, 21878, 21823, 21845, 21867];
const ES_PRICES = [5908, 5912, 5905, 5918, 5922, 5900, 5910, 5915];
let priceIdx = 0;

function fmtPnl(v) {
  const s = v >= 0 ? '+' : '';
  return s + '$' + Math.abs(v).toLocaleString('en-US', {minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2});
}
function setPnlEl(id, v) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  el.textContent = fmtPnl(v);
  el.style.color = v >= 0 ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
}

function resetPaper() {
  paper.balance = 50000; paper.rpnl = 0; paper.upnl = 0;
  paper.side = null; paper.entry = 0; paper.qty = 0;
  paper.wins = 0; paper.losses = 0; paper.closedTrades = 0;
  document.getElementById('paper-balance').textContent = '$150,000.00';
  document.getElementById('paper-upnl').textContent = '+$0.00';
  document.getElementById('paper-upnl').style.color = 'var(--green)';
  document.getElementById('paper-rpnl').textContent = '+$0.00';
  document.getElementById('paper-rpnl').style.color = 'var(--green)';
  document.getElementById('paper-winrate').textContent = '—';
  document.getElementById('paper-wl').textContent = '0W · 0L';
  document.getElementById('paper-side').textContent = 'FLAT';
  document.getElementById('paper-side').style.color = 'var(--text)';
  document.getElementById('paper-entry').textContent = 'No entry price';
  document.getElementById('paper-pos').textContent = 'No open position';
  document.getElementById('paper-trades-count').textContent = '0 trades closed';
  const log = document.getElementById('paper-log');
  log.innerHTML = '<tr id="paper-empty"><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);font-size:13px;padding:24px">No paper trades yet — connect a strategy to start receiving trades</td></tr>';
}

function updatePaperFromSignal(act, ticker, qty) {
  const prices = ticker === 'ES1!' ? ES_PRICES : NQ_PRICES;
  const currentPrice = prices[priceIdx % prices.length];
  const tickValue = ticker === 'ES1!' ? paper.ES_TICK : paper.NQ_TICK;
  priceIdx++;

  const d = new Date();
  const ts = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0')+':'+String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0')+':'+String(d.getSeconds()).padStart(2,'0');
  const actClass = act.startsWith('BUY') ? 'buy' : act.startsWith('SELL') ? 'sell' : 'close';
  const actLbl = act.replace('_LONG','').replace('_SHORT','');

  const empty = document.getElementById('paper-empty');
  if (empty) empty.remove();

  if (!paper.side) {
    // OPEN position
    if (act === 'BUY') { paper.side = 'LONG'; paper.entry = currentPrice; paper.qty = qty; }
    else if (act === 'SELL') { paper.side = 'SHORT'; paper.entry = currentPrice; paper.qty = qty; }
    else { return; } // close on flat = nothing

    document.getElementById('paper-side').textContent = paper.side;
    document.getElementById('paper-side').style.color = paper.side === 'LONG' ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
    document.getElementById('paper-entry').textContent = 'Entry: ' + paper.entry.toLocaleString();
    document.getElementById('paper-pos').textContent = paper.qty + 'x ' + ticker;

    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
    tr.id = 'paper-open-row';
    tr.innerHTML = `<td class="mono" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">${ts}</td><td><span class="badge ${actClass}">${actLbl}</span></td><td class="mono">${ticker}</td><td class="mono">${qty}</td><td class="mono">${paper.entry.toLocaleString()}</td><td class="mono" style="color:var(--text3)">—</td><td style="color:var(--text3)">Open</td><td><span class="badge paper">open</span></td>`;
    document.getElementById('paper-log').insertBefore(tr, document.getElementById('paper-log').firstChild);

    // Simulate unrealized move
    paper.upnl = (currentPrice + (paper.side === 'LONG' ? 4 : -4) - paper.entry) * tickValue * paper.qty;
    setPnlEl('paper-upnl', paper.upnl);

  } else {
    // CLOSE position
    const exitPrice = currentPrice;
    const pts = paper.side === 'LONG' ? exitPrice - paper.entry : paper.entry - exitPrice;
    const tradePnl = pts * tickValue * paper.qty;
    paper.rpnl += tradePnl;
    paper.balance += tradePnl;
    paper.upnl = 0;
    paper.closedTrades++;
    if (tradePnl >= 0) paper.wins++; else paper.losses++;

    // Update stats
    document.getElementById('paper-balance').textContent = '$' + paper.balance.toLocaleString('en-US', {minimumFractionDigits:2});
    setPnlEl('paper-rpnl', paper.rpnl);
    setPnlEl('paper-upnl', 0);
    document.getElementById('paper-trades-count').textContent = paper.closedTrades + ' trade' + (paper.closedTrades !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' closed';
    const wr = paper.closedTrades > 0 ? Math.round((paper.wins / paper.closedTrades) * 100) : 0;
    document.getElementById('paper-winrate').textContent = paper.closedTrades > 0 ? wr + '%' : '—';
    document.getElementById('paper-winrate').style.color = wr >= 50 ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
    document.getElementById('paper-wl').textContent = paper.wins + 'W · ' + paper.losses + 'L';
    document.getElementById('paper-side').textContent = 'FLAT';
    document.getElementById('paper-side').style.color = 'var(--text)';
    document.getElementById('paper-entry').textContent = 'No entry price';
    document.getElementById('paper-pos').textContent = 'No open position';

    // Update open row → closed
    const openRow = document.getElementById('paper-open-row');
    if (openRow) {
      const pnlColor = tradePnl >= 0 ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
      openRow.cells[4].textContent = paper.entry.toLocaleString();
      openRow.cells[5].textContent = exitPrice.toLocaleString();
      openRow.cells[6].innerHTML = `<span style="font-family:var(--mono);color:${pnlColor}">${fmtPnl(tradePnl)}</span>`;
      openRow.cells[7].innerHTML = tradePnl >= 0 ? '<span class="badge sent">win</span>' : '<span class="badge sell">loss</span>';
      openRow.removeAttribute('id');
    }
    paper.side = null; paper.entry = 0; paper.qty = 0;
  }
}

// Simulate signal
const ACTS=['BUY','SELL','CLOSE_LONG','CLOSE_SHORT'];
const TICKS=['NQ1!','ES1!'];
let sigN=14,ordN=42;
function simulate(){
  const act=ACTS[Math.floor(Math.random()*4)];
  const tick=TICKS[Math.floor(Math.random()*2)];
  const cls=act.startsWith('BUY')?'buy':act.startsWith('SELL')?'sell':'close';
  const lbl=act.replace('_LONG','').replace('_SHORT','');
  const d=new Date();
  const ts=`${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0')}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0')}:${String(d.getSeconds()).padStart(2,'0')}`;
  // Dash log
  const dl=document.getElementById('dash-log');
  const dr=document.createElement('tr');
  dr.innerHTML=`<td class="mono" style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">${ts}</td><td><span class="badge ${cls}">${lbl}</span></td><td class="mono">${tick}</td><td class="mono">2</td><td><span class="badge sent">sent</span></td>`;
  dl.insertBefore(dr,dl.firstChild);
  // Signal list
  const sl=document.getElementById('signal-list');
  const sr=document.createElement('div');
  sr.className='signal-row';
  sr.innerHTML=`<span class="s-time">03/13 ${ts} UTC</span><span class="s-act"><span class="badge ${cls}">${lbl}</span></span><span class="s-tick">${tick}</span><span class="s-qty">2x</span><span class="s-strat">NQ_Scalper v3 · MARKET</span><div class="s-subs"><div class="sub-dot ok">A</div><div class="sub-dot ok">M</div><div class="sub-dot ok">T</div></div>`;
  sl.insertBefore(sr,sl.firstChild);
  // Trades
  const tt=document.getElementById('trades-table');
  [['Alex T.','Tradovate','sent',2],['Maria C.','NinjaTrader','sent',1],['TestUser','Paper','paper',1]].forEach(([n,b,s,q])=>{
    const tr=document.createElement('tr');
    tr.innerHTML=`<td class="mono" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">${ts}</td><td class="mono">${n}</td><td><span class="badge ${cls}">${lbl}</span></td><td class="mono">${tick}</td><td class="mono">${q}</td><td style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text2)">${b}</td><td style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text3)">NQ_Scalper v3</td><td><span class="badge ${s}">${s}</span></td>`;
    tt.insertBefore(tr,tt.firstChild);
  });
  sigN++;ordN+=3;
  updatePaperFromSignal(act, tick, 1);
  document.getElementById('dc-sig').textContent=sigN;
  document.getElementById('dc-ord').textContent=ordN;
  document.getElementById('nb-sig').textContent=sigN;
}

// Connect demo from strategy page
let demoConnected = false;
let selectedDemoTier = '50k';
const demoTiers = {
  '50k':  { balance:50000, contract:'5x MNQ', contractShort:'5x MNQ', balanceFmt:'$50,000', qty:5, tickLabel:'MNQ', color:'var(--purple)', colorBg:'rgba(139,111,255,.06)', colorBorder:'rgba(139,111,255,.4)' },
  '100k': { balance:100000, contract:'8x MNQ', contractShort:'8x MNQ', balanceFmt:'$100,000', qty:8, tickLabel:'MNQ', color:'var(--amber)', colorBg:'rgba(240,176,64,.06)', colorBorder:'rgba(240,176,64,.4)' },
  '150k': { balance:150000, contract:'1x NQ', contractShort:'1x NQ', balanceFmt:'$150,000', qty:1, tickLabel:'NQ', color:'var(--accent)', colorBg:'rgba(0,200,240,.06)', colorBorder:'rgba(0,200,240,.4)' }
};

function selectDemoTier(tier){
  selectedDemoTier = tier;
  const tiers = ['50k','100k','150k'];
  tiers.forEach(t => {
    const opt = document.getElementById('demo-opt-'+t);
    const chk = document.getElementById('demo-check-'+t);
    if(t === tier){
      const d = demoTiers[t];
      opt.style.background = d.colorBg;
      opt.style.borderColor = d.colorBorder;
      chk.style.background = d.color;
      chk.style.border = 'none';
      chk.style.color = t==='150k' ? '#000' : '#fff';
      chk.innerHTML = '✓';
    } else {
      opt.style.background = 'var(--bg3)';
      opt.style.borderColor = 'var(--border)';
      chk.style.background = 'var(--bg4)';
      chk.style.border = '1px solid var(--border2)';
      chk.style.color = 'var(--text3)';
      chk.innerHTML = '';
    }
  });
}

  if(!requireSignup())return;
  document.getElementById('demo-connect-modal').classList.add('open');
}

function launchDemo(){
  const tier = demoTiers[selectedDemoTier];
  document.getElementById('demo-connect-modal').classList.remove('open');

  // Update paper balance display
  document.getElementById('paper-balance').textContent = tier.balanceFmt + '.00';
  document.getElementById('paper-balance').nextElementSibling.textContent = 'Starting: ' + tier.balanceFmt;

  // Toggle paper section to connected state
  document.getElementById('paper-not-connected').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('paper-connected').style.display = 'flex';

  // Update contract badge
  document.getElementById('paper-contract-badge').textContent = tier.contractShort;

  // Calculate expiry
  const expiry = new Date(); expiry.setDate(expiry.getDate()+30);
  const expiryStr = expiry.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'});
  document.getElementById('paper-expiry-badge').textContent = 'EXPIRES ' + expiryStr.toUpperCase();

  // Update status badge
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').textContent = 'STRATFORD ALPHA · 30-DAY DEMO';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').style.background = 'rgba(0,217,126,.1)';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').style.borderColor = 'rgba(0,217,126,.25)';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').style.color = 'var(--green)';

  // Persist demo activation to localStorage
  localStorage.setItem('sa_paper_demo', JSON.stringify({strategy:'Stratford Alpha', contract:tier.contractShort, balance:tier.balanceFmt, activated:new Date().toISOString()}));

  // Update dashboard active strategy card
  document.getElementById('dc-strat').textContent = 'Stratford Alpha';
  document.getElementById('dc-strat').style.color = 'var(--green)';
  document.getElementById('dc-strat-sub').textContent = tier.contractShort + ' · Paper Demo';
  document.getElementById('dc-broker').textContent = 'Paper';
  document.getElementById('dc-broker').parentElement.querySelector('.dd').textContent = tier.balanceFmt + ' demo account';

  // Switch to dashboard
  nav('dashboard',document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item')[0],'Dashboard');
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const paperSection = document.getElementById('paper-section');
    if(paperSection){
      paperSection.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});
      paperSection.querySelector('.panel').style.boxShadow='0 0 0 2px rgba(139,111,255,.6)';
      setTimeout(()=>{paperSection.querySelector('.panel').style.boxShadow='';},2000);
    }
  },200);
}

// Disconnect strategy from paper account
function disconnectStrategy(){
  demoConnected = false;
  document.getElementById('paper-not-connected').style.display = 'flex';
  document.getElementById('paper-connected').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').textContent = 'NOT CONNECTED';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').style.background = 'rgba(139,111,255,.1)';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').style.borderColor = 'rgba(139,111,255,.3)';
  document.getElementById('paper-status-badge').style.color = 'var(--purple)';
  // Clear dashboard active strategy card
  document.getElementById('dc-strat').textContent = '—';
  document.getElementById('dc-strat').style.color = '';
  document.getElementById('dc-strat-sub').textContent = 'No strategy connected';
  resetPaper();
}

// Subscribe modal
function openSubscribeModal(){
  if(!requireSignup())return;
  document.getElementById('subscribe-modal').classList.add('open');
}

function togglePlanPeriod(period, btn){
  const toggle = document.getElementById('plan-toggle');
  const buttons = toggle.querySelectorAll('button');
  buttons.forEach(b => { b.style.background='transparent'; b.style.color='var(--text2)'; });
  btn.style.background='var(--accent)'; btn.style.color='#000';

  document.querySelectorAll('.plan-price').forEach(el => {
    const price = period === 'yearly' ? el.dataset.yearly : el.dataset.monthly;
    el.textContent = '$' + price;
  });
}

function selectPlan(plan){
  document.getElementById('subscribe-modal').classList.remove('open');
  const names = {alpha:'Alpha ($99/mo)',pro:'Pro ($189/mo)',elite:'Elite ($250/mo)'};
  // Store selected plan on user
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(user){user.plan=plan;localStorage.setItem('sa_user',JSON.stringify(user));}
  alert('Plan selected: ' + names[plan] + '\n\nIn production this would redirect to Stripe checkout.\n\nAfter payment, you\'ll be able to connect your live broker.');
  nav('brokers',document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item')[5],'Brokers › Connect Broker');
}

// Gate affiliate page behind Pro or Elite subscription
function gateAffiliate(el){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(user && (user.plan==='pro' || user.plan==='elite')){
    nav('affiliate',el,'Affiliate Program');
  } else {
    alert('The Affiliate Program is available for Pro ($189/mo) and Elite ($250/mo) subscribers.\n\nUpgrade your plan to unlock referral earnings.');
    openSubscribeModal();
  }
}

// Gate live broker connections behind subscription
const _origOpenBrokerModal = openBrokerModal;
openBrokerModal = function(name){
  if(name === 'Paper Account'){
    _origOpenBrokerModal(name);
  } else {
    openSubscribeModal();
  }
};

function seededRandom(seed){let s=seed;return function(){s=(s*16807)%2147483647;return(s-1)/2147483646;};}

function generateReviews(count){
  const rng=seededRandom(42);
  const reviews=[];
  const accs=['$50K','$100K','$150K'];
  const plans=['Alpha','Pro','Elite'];
  const prices=['99','189','250'];
  const tiers=['5x MNQ','8x MNQ','1x NQ'];
  const earns=['2,400','3,800','5,200','1,900','4,100','6,500','3,200','2,800','4,600','7,100'];
  const wrs=['70','71','72','73','69','74','68'];
  for(let i=0;i<count;i++){
    const tmpl=reviewTemplates[Math.floor(rng()*reviewTemplates.length)];
    const fn=reviewFirstNames[Math.floor(rng()*reviewFirstNames.length)];
    const li=reviewLastInits[Math.floor(rng()*reviewLastInits.length)];
    const city=reviewCities[Math.floor(rng()*reviewCities.length)];
    const ai=Math.floor(rng()*3);
    const pi=Math.floor(rng()*3);
    let body=tmpl.b.replace(/\{name\}/g,'Stratford Alpha').replace(/\{acc\}/g,accs[ai]).replace(/\{plan\}/g,plans[pi]).replace(/\{price\}/g,prices[pi]).replace(/\{tier\}/g,tiers[ai]).replace(/\{earn\}/g,earns[Math.floor(rng()*earns.length)]).replace(/\{wr\}/g,wrs[Math.floor(rng()*wrs.length)]).replace(/\{trades\}/g,'4,154');
    const daysAgo=Math.floor(rng()*900);
    const d=new Date();d.setDate(d.getDate()-daysAgo);
    const tag=tmpl.tag||reviewTags[Math.floor(rng()*reviewTags.length)];
    const stars=tmpl.s||(rng()>0.15?5:4);
    const helpful=Math.floor(rng()*60);
    reviews.push({name:fn+' '+li+'.',city:city,stars:stars,title:tmpl.t,body:body,date:d,daysAgo:daysAgo,tag:tag,helpful:helpful,avatar:fn[0]+li[0]});
  }
  reviews.sort((a,b)=>a.daysAgo-b.daysAgo);
  return reviews;
}

const allReviews=generateReviews(520);
let reviewPage=0;
const reviewsPerPage=20;
let currentFilter='all';

function renderReviewCard(r){
  const stars='★'.repeat(r.stars)+(r.stars<5?'<span style="color:var(--text3)">'+'☆'.repeat(5-r.stars)+'</span>':'');
  const monthNames=['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
  const timeAgo=r.daysAgo===0?'Today':r.daysAgo===1?'Yesterday':r.daysAgo<7?r.daysAgo+' days ago':r.daysAgo<30?Math.floor(r.daysAgo/7)+' weeks ago':r.daysAgo<90?Math.floor(r.daysAgo/30)+' months ago':monthNames[r.date.getMonth()]+' '+r.date.getDate()+', '+r.date.getFullYear();
  const tagHtml=r.tag==='prop'?'<span style="background:rgba(139,111,255,.1);border:1px solid rgba(139,111,255,.25);border-radius:3px;color:var(--purple);font-family:var(--mono);font-size:9px;padding:2px 6px">PROP FIRM</span>':r.tag==='beginner'?'<span style="background:rgba(0,217,126,.1);border:1px solid rgba(0,217,126,.25);border-radius:3px;color:var(--green);font-family:var(--mono);font-size:9px;padding:2px 6px">BEGINNER</span>':'';
  return `<div class="panel" style="padding:18px 20px" data-stars="${r.stars}" data-tag="${r.tag}">
    <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:10px">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
        <div style="width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:50%;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(0,184,230,.2),rgba(139,111,255,.2));display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-family:var(--mono);font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);flex-shrink:0">${r.avatar}</div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">${r.name} ${tagHtml}</div>
          <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">${r.city}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:right;flex-shrink:0">
        <div style="color:var(--amber);font-size:12px">${stars}</div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:2px">${timeAgo}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:6px">${r.title}</div>
    <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6">${r.body}</div>
    <div style="margin-top:12px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between">
      <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">👍 ${r.helpful} people found this helpful</div>
      <button onclick="helpfulReview(this)" style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;padding:5px 12px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text2);cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--sans);transition:all .15s" onmouseover="this.style.borderColor='var(--accent)';this.style.color='var(--accent)'" onmouseout="if(!this.classList.contains('voted')){this.style.borderColor='var(--border)';this.style.color='var(--text2)'}">👍 Helpful</button>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function helpfulReview(btn){
  if(btn.classList.contains('voted'))return;
  btn.classList.add('voted');
  const row=btn.parentElement;
  const countDiv=row.querySelector('div');
  const match=countDiv.textContent.match(/(\d+)/);
  if(match)countDiv.textContent='👍 '+(parseInt(match[1])+1)+' people found this helpful';
  btn.textContent='✓ Voted';
  btn.style.borderColor='var(--accent)';
  btn.style.color='var(--accent)';
  btn.style.background='rgba(0,200,240,.06)';
}
function loadReviewsPage(){
  const container=document.getElementById('reviews-container');
  const filtered=currentFilter==='all'?allReviews:currentFilter==='5'||currentFilter==='4'?allReviews.filter(r=>r.stars==currentFilter):allReviews.filter(r=>r.tag===currentFilter);
  const start=0;
  const end=(reviewPage+1)*reviewsPerPage;
  const slice=filtered.slice(start,end);
  container.innerHTML=slice.map(renderReviewCard).join('');
  const btn=document.getElementById('load-more-btn');
  const countEl=document.getElementById('reviews-shown-count');
  if(end>=filtered.length){btn.style.display='none';}else{btn.style.display='';}
  countEl.textContent='Showing '+Math.min(end,filtered.length)+' of '+filtered.length+' reviews';
}

function loadMoreReviews(){reviewPage++;loadReviewsPage();}

function filterReviews(filter,btn){
  currentFilter=filter;
  reviewPage=0;
  document.querySelectorAll('#page-reviews .ftab').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  loadReviewsPage();
}

    const timeAgo=r.daysAgo<7?r.daysAgo+' days ago':r.daysAgo<30?Math.floor(r.daysAgo/7)+' weeks ago':r.daysAgo<90?Math.floor(r.daysAgo/30)+' months ago':mn[r.date.getMonth()]+' '+r.date.getDate()+', '+r.date.getFullYear();
    return `<div style="min-width:260px;max-width:260px;background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:14px 16px;scroll-snap-align:start;flex-shrink:0">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-bottom:8px">

        <div style="flex:1;min-width:0"><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:500;color:var(--text);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${r.name}</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">${r.city}</div></div>
        <div style="color:var(--amber);font-size:9px;flex-shrink:0">${'★'.repeat(r.stars)}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:4px;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${r.title}</div>
      <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5;display:-webkit-box;-webkit-line-clamp:2;-webkit-box-orient:vertical;overflow:hidden">${r.body}</div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:6px">${timeAgo}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

// Init reviews on page load
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){renderDashTestimonials();renderLeaderboard();loadReviewsPage();renderCalendar();renderMiniCal();initTrialCountdown();});

function initTrialCountdown(){
  const user=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sa_user')||'null');
  if(!user||!user.signedUp) return;
  if(user.plan==='alpha'||user.plan==='pro'||user.plan==='elite') return;
  const bar=document.getElementById('trial-countdown-bar');
  bar.style.display='block';
  const signupDate=new Date(user.date||Date.now());
  const expiry=new Date(signupDate.getTime()+30*24*60*60*1000);
  function tick(){
    const now=new Date();
    const diff=expiry-now;
    const d=Math.max(0,Math.ceil(diff/86400000));
    const daysEl=document.getElementById('trial-cd-days');
    const textEl=document.getElementById('trial-days-text');
    daysEl.textContent=d;
    if(d<=0){textEl.textContent='— Expired';textEl.style.color='var(--red)';daysEl.style.color='var(--red)';}
    else{textEl.textContent='day'+(d!==1?'s':'')+' left';
      if(d<=3){daysEl.style.color='var(--red)';}
      else if(d<=7){daysEl.style.color='var(--amber)';}
      else{daysEl.style.color='var(--accent)';}
    }
    const pct=Math.max(0,Math.min(100,(diff/(30*24*60*60*1000))*100));
    document.getElementById('trial-progress-bar').style.width=pct+'%';
  }
  tick();
  setInterval(tick,60000);
}

// Trade filters
let tradeFilterPeriod='all';
function filterTrades(type,btn,val){
  if(type==='period'){
    tradeFilterPeriod=val;
    btn.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.trade-filter-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
    btn.classList.add('active');
  }
  applyTradeFilters();
}
function applyTradeFilters(){
  // Filters are ready — when real trades exist they'll filter the trades-table rows
  // For now just update the count display
  const rows=document.querySelectorAll('#trades-table tr:not([id])');
  const total=rows.length;
  const el=document.getElementById('trades-result-count');
  if(el)el.textContent=total>0?total+' trades':'0 trades';
}
function exportTrades(){
  alert('Trade export will be available when you have executed trades.');
}

function toggleSidebar(){
  document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.toggle('open');
  document.getElementById('sidebar-overlay').classList.toggle('open');
}

function closeSidebarMobile(){
  if(window.innerWidth<=768){
    document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('sidebar-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  }
}

function toggleStratCard(header){
  const body = header.parentElement.querySelector('.strat-card-body');
  const chev = header.querySelector('.strat-card-chev');
  const isOpen = body.style.maxHeight && body.style.maxHeight !== '0px';
  body.style.maxHeight = isOpen ? '0px' : body.scrollHeight + 'px';
  if(chev) chev.style.transform = isOpen ? '' : 'rotate(180deg)';
}

function toggleTheme(){
  const html = document.documentElement;
  const isDark = html.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'light';
  html.setAttribute('data-theme', isDark ? 'light' : 'dark');
  const btn = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
  btn.innerHTML = isDark ? '🌙' : '☀️';
  btn.title = isDark ? 'Switch to dark mode' : 'Switch to light mode';
  localStorage.setItem('theme', isDark ? 'light' : 'dark');
}
// Load saved theme
(function(){
  const saved = localStorage.getItem('theme');
  if(saved === 'light'){
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme','light');
    const btn = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
    if(btn){ btn.innerHTML = '🌙'; btn.title = 'Switch to dark mode'; }
  }
})();
</script>

<!-- Floating theme toggle -->
<button id="theme-toggle" onclick="toggleTheme()" title="Switch to light mode" style="
  position:fixed;bottom:24px;right:24px;z-index:999;
  width:48px;height:48px;border-radius:50%;border:1px solid var(--border2);
  background:var(--bg2);color:var(--text);font-size:20px;
  cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;
  box-shadow:0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,.4);
  transition:all .3s;backdrop-filter:blur(8px);
">☀️</button>
